She also reports significant mucus in the morning that causes her to vomit. Patient denies any fever. She has had cough but it's been nonproductive. Patient reports no fevers or lower extremity swelling. Patient reports no history of smoking or pulmonary disease.  Patient's initial pulse ox was 78% on room air. Patient's lungs had rales in the posterior right base. Patient was afebrile. Oxygen saturation is 95% on 3 L after breathing treatment was administered. Patient no lower extremity swelling was afebrile. Patient did have labs obtained from her primary care doctor yesterday. Chest x-ray showed some cephalization as well as bibasilar infiltrate as read by the radiologist with the differential being multifocal pneumonia versus edema. Patient's BNP yesterday was 160s. Patient's white blood cell count was 9 yesterday however there was a left shift. Patient at this time was given a breathing treatment which she reports moderately improved her symptoms. Patient has no history of congestive heart failure. At this time, labs demonstrated BNP of 200. Patient also had an elevation of her white blood cell count at 13,000. While the clinical situation is not entirely clear, blood cultures and lactate were obtained and patient was given antibiotics for community-acquired pneumonia.  Patient was also given a small amount of Lasix secondary to the fact that she is Lasix naïve as well as given Nitropaste for possible underlying edema.
